\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"webhook returned invalid response.patchType of %q\", patchType)\n80: \t\t\t\t}\n81: \t\t\t}\n82: \t\t} else {\n83: \t\t\t// Ensure a validating webhook doesn't       r.Response.Result,\n98: \t\t\tWarnings:         r.Response.Warnings,\n99: \t\t}, nil\n100: \n101: \tcase *admissionv1beta1.AdmissionReview:\n102: \t\tif r.Response == nil {\n103: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"webhook response was absent\")\n104: \t\t}\n105: \n106: \t\t// Response GVK and response.uid were not verified in v1beta1 handling, allow any\n107: \n108: \t\tpatch := []byte(nil)\n109: \t\tpatchType := admissionv1.PatchType(\"\")\n110: \t\tif mutating {\n111: \t\t\tpatch = r.Response.Patch\n112: \t\t\tif len(r.Response.Patch) > 0 {\n113: \t\t\t\t// patch type was not verified in v1beta1 admissionreview handling. pin to only supported version if a patch is provided.\n114: \t\t\t\tpatchType = admissionv1.PatchTypeJSONPatch\n115: \t\t\t}\n116: \t\t}\n117: \n118:       patchType,\n123: \t\t\tResult:           r.Response.Result,\n124: \t\t\tWarnings:         r.Response.Warnings,\n125: \t\t}, nil\n126: \n127: \tdefault:\n128: \t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected response type %T\", review)\n129: \t}\n130: }\n131: \n132: // CreateAdmissionObjects returns the unique request uid, the AdmissionReview object to send the webhook and to The `Dispatch()` method orchestrates the process: it checks if the request should call webhooks, retrieves the list of active webhooks from the hook source (configuration manager), and then delegates to the dispatcher.\\n\\n   Key methods:\\n   - `Dispatch()`: Entry point for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n   - `ShouldCallHook()`: Determines if a webhook should be called based on namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n2. **Generic Webhook Interfaces** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go`): Defines the `Dispatcher` interface that both mutating and validating dispatchers implement.\\n\\n3. **Mutating Webhook Dispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`): Implements sequential webhook dispatch for mutating webhooks. Pre-filters relevant webhooks based on matching rules\\n   - Spawns goroutines for parallel webhook calls using `callHook()`\\n   - Aggregates errors from all webhook calls\\n   - Returns the first error encountered\\n\\n## Admission Response Aggregation\\n\\nThe response handling and aggregation is implemented in multiple places:\\n\\n1. **AdmissionReview Request/Response Handling** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go`):\\n   - Calls the webhook via REST client\\n   - Verifies the admission response using `VerifyAdmissionResponse()`\\n   - Applies JSON patches to the object\\n   - Adds audit annotations for mutations and patches\\n   - Implements caching for compiled matchers and REST clients.\\n\\n2. **Error Handling** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/statuserror.go`): The `ToStatusErr()` function converts webhook rejections to proper Kubernetes status errors.\\n\\n3. **Configuration Managers**:\\n   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n\\n4. **Initializer** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/initializer/initializer.go`): Initializes webhook plugins with necessary dependencies.\\n\\n5. **Match Conditions** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go`): Handles CEL-based match conditions for webhook invocation filtering.\\n\\n6. **Reinvocation Context** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`): Manages webhook reinvocation for mutating webhooks when mutations change the request object.\\n\\n## Call Flow Summary\\n\\n1. The chain consists of three main components: the webhook admission controller, the webhook call dispatch mechanism, and the admission response aggregation.\\n\\n## Webhook Admission Controllers\\n\\nThe entry points for the admission webhook chain are the MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugins:\\n\\n1. **MutatingAdmissionWebhook Plugin** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`): This plugin implements the `admission.MutationInterface`. The `Admit()` method is called by the API server to apply mutations to incoming requests. It delegates to the generic webhook's `Dispatch()` method.\\n\\n2. **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook Plugin** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`): This plugin implements the `admission.ValidationInterface`. The `Validate()` method is called by the API server to validate incoming requests. It also delegates to the generic webhook's `Dispatch()` method.\\n\\n## Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nThe dispatch mechanism is implemented in the generic webhook and specific dispatcher implementations:\\n\\n1. **Generic Webhook** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`): This is the core controller that manages the entire webhook lifecycle. The `Dispatch()` method orchestrates the process: it checks if the request should call webhooks, retrieves the list of active webhooks from the hook source (configuration manager), and then delegates to the dispatcher.\\n\\n   Key methods:\\n   - `Dispatch()`: Entry point for both mutating and validating webhooks\\n   - `ShouldCallHook()`: Determines if a webhook should be called based on namespace selectors, object selectors, rules, and match conditions\\n\\n2. **Generic Webhook Interfaces** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go`): Defines the `Dispatcher` interface that both mutating and validating dispatchers implement.\\n\\n3. **Mutating Webhook Dispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`): Implements sequential webhook dispatch for mutating webhooks. Key features:\\n   - Loops through hooks sequentially\\n   - Calls `callAttrMutatingHook()` for each webhook\\n   - Handles patch application and reinvocation\\n   - Supports reinvocation policy for webhooks marked as eligible\\n   - Manages audit annotations for mutations and patches\\n\\n4. **Validating Webhook Dispatcher** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`): Implements parallel webhook dispatch for validating webhooks:\\n   - Pre-filters relevant webhooks based on matching rules\\n   - Spawns goroutines for parallel webhook calls using `callHook()`\\n   - Aggregates errors from all webhook calls\\n   - Returns the first error encountered\\n\\n## Admission Response Aggregation\\n\\nThe response handling and aggregation is implemented in multiple places:\\n\\n1. **AdmissionReview Request/Response Handling** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go`):\\n   - `CreateAdmissionObjects()`: Creates AdmissionReview request objects in both v1 and v1beta1 formats\\n   - `CreateV1AdmissionReview()` and `CreateV1beta1AdmissionReview()`: Construct properly formatted admission requests\\n   - `VerifyAdmissionResponse()`: Validates webhook responses, extracts audit annotations, warnings, patches, and status information\\n\\n2. **Mutating Webhook Dispatcher Response Handling**: The `callAttrMutatingHook()` method in mutating/dispatcher.go:\\n   - Calls the webhook via REST client\\n   - Verifies the admission response using `VerifyAdmissionResponse()`\\n   - Applies JSON patches to the object\\n   - Adds audit annotations for mutations and patches\\n   - Returns rejection status if webhook denies the request\\n\\n3. **Validating Webhook Dispatcher Response Handling**: The `callHook()` method in validating/dispatcher.go:\\n   - Calls the webhook via REST client\\n   - Verifies the admission response\\n   - Extracts audit annotations and warnings\\n   - Returns rejection error if webhook denies the request\\n   - Parallel calls are aggregated with the first error being returned\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n\\n1. **WebhookAccessor** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`): Provides a unified interface for accessing mutating and validating webhook configurations. Implements caching for compiled matchers and REST clients.\\n\\n2. **Error Handling** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/errors/statuserror.go`): The `ToStatusErr()` function converts webhook rejections to proper Kubernetes status errors.\\n\\n3. **Configuration Managers**:\\n   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n   - `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go`: Manages ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n\\n4. **Initializer** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/initializer/initializer.go`): Initializes webhook plugins with necessary dependencies.\\n\\n5. **Match Conditions** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go`): Handles CEL-based match conditions for webhook invocation filtering.\\n\\n6. **Reinvocation Context** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`): Manages webhook reinvocation for mutating webhooks when mutations change the request object.\\n\\n## Call Flow Summary\\n\\n1. API server calls `Admit()` (mutating) or `Validate()` (validating) on the plugin\\n2. Plugin delegates to `Webhook.Dispatch()`\\n3. `Dispatch()` checks if webhooks should be called and retrieves the webhook list\\n4. Dispatcher's `Dispatch()` is called with the hook list\\n5. For each matching hook, the dispatcher calls the webhook via REST client\\n6. `CreateAdmissionObjects()` creates the AdmissionReview request\\n7. Webhook response is verified with `VerifyAdmissionResponse()`\\n8. For mutating webhooks: patches are applied and mutations are tracked\\n9. For validating webhooks: multiple calls are made in parallel and errors are aggregated\\n10. Final decision and audit annotations are returned to the API server\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
